< Text>
Hmmmmm....I'm torn on Cox Cable.

I only have 2 choices for cable where I live, and neither is on my good list. Since we are talking about Cox, we'll focus on them.

< Review>
Not sure if anyone here is actually rating the store rather than the company as a whole but...

So far I have had generally positive experiences here, and I don't come often because I like to deal with my bills over the phone when it comes to sudden charges or bundle discounts. They just seem more equipped for that stuff.

As for the store, I have come in to return/replace equipment, and add new services.

If the service reps that handled my modem upgrade didn't mess up the Mac address input twice, I would have given the location 5 stars. I also only knocked out one star because it's happened only twice in the many years this place has been here.

*** Review *** (My recent experience that warranted the 4 star review)

In November 2016 I decided to upgrade my cable modem since I had been renting for a couple years. I brought in a compatible modem from a local retailer to the store so they could add it to my account. The sales rep suggested I purchased a modem that they offered in store since it was faster and cheaper than what I had purchased. Since I financed it I refused, and the rep seemed to dislike my choice since he changed the tone of his voice and was kinda rude towards the end of the transaction. Though I won't lie, he had a point.

Anyway, I got home and installed the new hardware and it wasn't connecting so I called Cox's trusty customer service line and found out that the rep input an incorrect Mac address (the "serial number" required by Cox in order to send your devices an internet connection).

*** End Review ***

This part doesn't have a whole lot to do with the review but it just kinda frustrates me because I actually went back to purchase the modem that the sales rep suggested to me since it really was a better investment for my money.

What a sucker right??

Well, after having the modem for 3 months it started to constantly disconnect all of my devices. I've gone through several technicians and a full rewiring of the house only to find out that the modem I bought was a lemon.

So ill be going to the store today to see if they will take it back and credit it towards my bill since I spent basically a whole month's worth of service for it. Not to mention dealing with the technicians (Don't get a technician on the weekends... you'll likely get a 3rd party contractor and my experience with those guys sucked.)

I was patient... nicer than I should have been too... and also a loyal 8 year customer... so I'd like to say I'm good for it. Heck, the modem still looks brand new and has original packaging! If the return experience will help someone else, I'll add it to this review.<//Review>

< Review>
Out of all the poke places in Bakersfield, this is by far the best one! Food, Atmosphere, and Service were all top notch.

Atmosphere - very clean, may seem small but there is plenty of seating inside and out

Service - super friendly and welcoming. First time? no problem, they were more than happy to answer any questions. Most people get their food to-go, and you're in and out very quick

Food - for me, this is the main reason they deserve 5 stars. Overall quality of the food [salmon, shrimp, etc.] is fresh, as well as the toppings. I don't do raw, and specifically the shrimp is bigger than all the other poke places in town. My sister [who does eat raw] ordered the salmon and she also says the fish was more fresh than the last poke place we ate at (SWP). I forgot to mention that the amount of portions they give you is also more than the other poke joints for the same price (SWP)

You won't be disappointed in trying this place out, and if I'm wrong, try the other places and I'm sure you'll be coming back to this place. Oh yeah, if you think it's too overpriced; I'd rather pay more for quality than quantity<//Review>

<text>My doctor talked me into start running but I‚Äôve never owned a pair of actually running shoes before.  I also have flat feet from genetics.  And wearing flip flops for the past decade probably didn‚Äôt help so I wanted some advice.  I read some great reviews for this place and saw they had a foot scanner.  The scanner not only measured my foot size very precisely (12.9 for my left foot and 13.2 for my right foot) but also showed my arch measurements.  Very cool stuff!

The customer service was great there as well.  There was another gentleman in there trying on shoes and Vincent was the only one working at the time.  He came over to welcome me and introduce himself real quick and then went back to finish helping the guy.  After a few minutes he checked the man out at the register and then came to help me.  I‚Äôm very good at spotting a ‚Äúsalesman‚Äù within a few seconds and I hate pressure to buy.  Vincent was very easy going and genuinely seemed like he wanted to help.  I never felt any pressure to buy anything.  He also told me they have a 60 day return policy even if I‚Äôve run in them so that was also a big plus.

The shoe selection there was pretty good and I compared a few of the prices to amazon.  The pairs I checked were the same prices I found online.  Vincent even told me to go check out the clearance section before I made a decision.

Ok so the foot scanner said I needed some inserts and Vincent brought out a couple different options to try.  I settled on a set and he cut them to fit the shoes I found.  Just a heads up though, the inserts were not cheap.  Mine were $60.  You can definitely tell they‚Äôre there, but since I‚Äôve never really worn running shoes or shoes with inserts, I‚Äôm not sure how it‚Äôs supposed to feel.  I‚Äôve been running a few miles in them and my feet don‚Äôt hurt so I guess they‚Äôre working.
